grade60"><rb>英文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>영문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로는 armistice라 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>稱</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>칭</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하나, <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이라 한다.
</p>
<h2><span id="締結(체결)_過程(과정)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.B7.A0.E7.B5.90.28.EC.B2.B4.EA.B2.B0.29_.E9.81.8E.E7.A8.8B.28.EA.B3.BC.EC.A0.95.29"><ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>締結</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>체결</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>過程</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>과정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="부분 편집: 締結(체결) 過程(과정)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h2><span id="朝鮮文(조선문)_文本(문본)_內容(내용)[1]"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E6.9C.9D.E9.AE.AE.E6.96.87.28.EC.A1.B0.EC.84.A0.EB.AC.B8.29_.E6.96.87.E6.9C.AC.28.EB.AC.B8.EB.B3.B8.29_.E5.85.A7.E5.AE.B9.28.EB.82.B4.EC.9A.A9.29.5B1.5D"><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>文本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>內容</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>내용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="부분 편집: 朝鮮文(조선문) 文本(문본) 內容(내용)[1]">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="序言(서언)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E5.BA.8F.E8.A8.80.28.EC.84.9C.EC.96.B8.29"><ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>序言</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>서언</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="부분 편집: 序言(서언)">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>人民軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인민군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>最高</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>최고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>人民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>志願軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지원군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>一方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 하고 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>聯合國軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>연합국군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>련합국군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>總</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>총</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 다른 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>一方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 하는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>下記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>하기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>署名者</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>서명자</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들은 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>莫大</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>막대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>苦痛</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>고통</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>流血</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>유혈</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>류혈</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>招來</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>초래</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>衝突</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>충돌</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停止</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정지</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>시키기 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>爲</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여서와 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>最後的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>최후적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>인 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>平和的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>평화적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解決</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해결</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>達成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>달성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>될 때까지 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에서의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>行爲</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>행위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>一切</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일절</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>行動</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>행동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>完全</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>완전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停止</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정지</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>保障</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>確立</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>확립</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>目的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>목적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>下記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>하기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>條項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>記載</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기재</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>된 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條件</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조건</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>接受</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>접수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 또 그 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>制約</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제약</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>統制</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 받는데 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各自</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각자</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>互相</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>호상</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>同意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  이 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條件</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조건</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>意圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>의도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>純全</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>순전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>히 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>軍事的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>性質</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>성질</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>屬</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 것이며 이는 오직 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에서의 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>交戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>교전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에만 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>適用</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p>
<h3><span id="第(제)1條(조)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.291.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>1<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="부분 편집: 第(제)1條(조)">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><big><b><ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>分界線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>분계선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>非武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>地帶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></b></big>
</p><p>1. 한<ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>個</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>개</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>分界線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>분계선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>確定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>확정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하고 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 이 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로부터 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>各其</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>二</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(2) 키로 메터씩 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>後退</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>후퇴</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>함으로써 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>軍隊間</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군대간</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 한<ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>個</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>개</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>非武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>地帶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>設定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>설정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  한<ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>個</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>개</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>非武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>地帶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>設定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>설정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>緩衝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>완충</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>地帶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 함으로써 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>行爲</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>행위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>再發</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>재발</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>招來</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>초래</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 수 있는 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>事件</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사건</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>發生</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>발생</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>防止</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>방지</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>2. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>分界線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>분계선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>位置</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위치</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>添附</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>첨부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>地圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>標示</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>표시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 바와 같다 (<ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>添附</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>첨부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>地圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>1<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 보라)
</p><p>3. <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>非武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>地帶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>添附</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>첨부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>地圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>標示</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>표시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>北</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>북</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>境界線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>경계선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>南</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>남</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>境界線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>경계선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로써 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>確定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>확정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다 (<ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>添附</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>첨부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>地圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>1<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 보라)
</p><p>4. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>分界線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>분계선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja <h3><span id="第(제)2條(조)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.292.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>2<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="부분 편집: 第(제)2條(조)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><big><b><ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停火</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정화</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;및 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>具體的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구체적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>措置</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조치</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></b></big>
</p>
<h4><span id="가._總則(총칙)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".EA.B0.80._.E7.B8.BD.E5.89.87.28.EC.B4.9D.EC.B9.99.29">가. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>總則</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>총칙</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="부분 편집: 가. 總則(총칙)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>12. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>十二</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>십이</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(12) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>時間</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시간</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>全體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>徹底</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>철저</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>히 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>遵守</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>준수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 것을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>保障</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들은 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>互相</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>호상</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>積極</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적극</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協力</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협력</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>積極</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적극</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協力</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협력</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>함으로써 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>全體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>文句</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>精神</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정신</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>遵守</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>준수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하도록 한다
</p><p>18. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 그 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各自</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각자</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>屬</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>事業</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사업</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>費用</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>均等</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>균등</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하게 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>負擔</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부담</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p>
<h4><span id="나._軍事(군사)_停戰(정전)_委員會(위원회)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".EB.82.98._.E8.BB.8D.E4.BA.8B.28.EA.B5.B0.EC.82.AC.29_.E5.81.9C.E6.88.B0.28.EC.A0.95.EC.A0.84.29_.E5.A7.94.E5.93.A1.E6.9C.83.28.EC.9C.84.EC.9B.90.ED.9A.8C.29">나. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="부분 편집: 나. 軍事(군사) 停戰(정전) 委員會(위원회)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span id="1._構成(구성)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1._.E6.A7.8B.E6.88.90.28.EA.B5.AC.EC.84.B1.29">1. <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>構成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="부분 편집: 1. 構成(구성)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>19. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>設立</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>설립</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>20. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>十</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>십</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(10) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>高級</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>고급</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>軍官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>構成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하되 그 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>五</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>오</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(5) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>人民軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인민군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>最高</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>최고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>人民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>志願軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지원군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>任命</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 그 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>五</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>오</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(5) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>聯合國軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>연합국군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>련합국군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>總</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>총</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>任命</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>十</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>십</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(10) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에서 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>三</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>삼</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(3) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>將領級</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>장령급</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>屬</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여야 하며 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 남아지 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>二</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(2) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>少將</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>准將</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>준장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>大佐</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대좌</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>或</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>혹</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 그와 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>同級</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동급</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>인 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>者</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>자</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 할 수 있다
</p><p>21. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 그 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>必要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>필요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 따라 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>參謀</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>참모</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>補助</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>人員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>使用</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할수 있다
</p><p>22. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>必要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>필요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>行政</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>행정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>人員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>配置</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>배치</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>祕書處</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비서처</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>設置</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>설치</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하되 그 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>任務</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임무</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>記錄</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기록</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>書記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>서기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>通譯</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통역</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>指定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>其他</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기타</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>職責</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>직책</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>執行</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>집행</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協助</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 것이다  <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>各其</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>祕書處</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비서처</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>祕書長</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비서장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>一</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(1) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>補助</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>祕書長</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비서장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>一</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(1) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>祕書處</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비서처</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>必要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>필요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>書記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>서기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>專門</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>技術</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기술</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>人員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>任命</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>記錄</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기록</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>中國文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중국문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>英文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>영문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>作成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>작성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하되 세가지 글은 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>同等</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동등</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>效力</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>효력</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 가진다
</p><p>23. ㄱ. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 처음에는 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>十</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>십</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(10) <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>個</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>개</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監視</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 두어 그 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協助</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 받는다  <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>數</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>首席</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수석</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>合意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>합의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 거처 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>減少</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감소</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 수 있다
</p><p>ㄴ. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>每個</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>매개</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監視</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>四</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(4) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>乃至</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>내지</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>六</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>육</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>륙</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(6) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>佐級</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>좌급</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>軍官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>構成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하되 그 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>半數</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>반수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>人民軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인민군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>最高</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>최고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>人民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>志願軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지원군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>任命</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 그 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>半數</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>반수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>聯合國軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>연합국군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>련합국군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>總</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>총</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>任命</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監視</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>事業上</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사업상</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>必要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>필요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>運轉手</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>운전수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>書記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>서기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>通譯</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통역</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>等</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>등</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>附屬</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>人員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>提供</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제공</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p>
<h5><span id="2._職責(직책)과_權限(권한)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2._.E8.81.B7.E8.B2.AC.28.EC.A7.81.EC.B1.85.29.EA.B3.BC_.E6.AC.8A.E9.99.90.28.EA.B6.8C.ED.95.9C.29">2. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>職責</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>직책</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>權限</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>권한</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="부분 편집: 2. 職責(직책)과 權限(권한)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>24. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>全般的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전반적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>任務</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임무</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>實施</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>실시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 어떠한 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>違反</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위반</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>事件</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사건</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이던지 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>處理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>처리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 것이다
</p><p>25. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는
</p><p>ㄱ. <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本部</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>板門店</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>판문점</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(<ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>北緯</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>북위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 37<ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>度</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 57<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>分</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>분</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 29<ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>秒</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>초</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>東經</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동경</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 126<ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>度</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 40<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>分</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>분</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 00<ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>秒</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>초</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>) <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>附近</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부근</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>設置</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>설치</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>首席</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수석</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>合意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>합의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 거처 그 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本部</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>非武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>地帶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>內</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>내</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 다른 한 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>地點</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지점</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>移設</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이설</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 수 있다
</p><p>ㄴ. <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>機構</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로서 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>事業</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사업</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>進行</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>진행</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>議長</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>의장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 두지 않는다
</p><p>ㄷ. 그가 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>隨時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>必要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>필요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하다고 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>認定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>節次</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>절차</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>採擇</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>채택</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>ㄹ. <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>非武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>地帶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>漢江</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>한강</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>河口</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>하구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>執行</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>집행</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>ㅁ. <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監視</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>事業</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사업</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>指導</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>ㅂ. <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 어떠한 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>違反</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위반</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>事件</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사건</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이던지 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>處理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>처리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>ㅅ. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로부터 받은 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>違反</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위반</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>事件</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사건</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>一切</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일절</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>調査</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>一切</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일절</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>其他</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기타</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>會議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>회의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>記錄</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기록</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>卽時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>즉시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들에게 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>傳達</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전달</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>ㅇ. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>下記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>하기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 바와 같이 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>設立</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>설립</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>失鄕</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>실향</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>私民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>歸鄕</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>귀향</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協助</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>事業</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사업</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>全般的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전반적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>指導</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>ㅈ. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>間</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>간</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>通信</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통신</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>傳達</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전달</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>仲介</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중개</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>役割</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>역할</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>擔當</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>담당</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>但</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>단</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>上記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>상기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들이 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>使用</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하고저 하는 어떠한 다른 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>方法</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>방법</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>使用</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>互相</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>호상</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>通信</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통신</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>傳達</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전달</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 것을 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>排除</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>배제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 것으로 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>解釋</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해석</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 수 없다
</p><p>ㅊ. 그의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>工作</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공작</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>人員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 그의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監視</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>證明</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>증명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>文件</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문건</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade12"><rb>徽章</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>휘장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 또 그 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>任務</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임무</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>執行時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>집행시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>使用</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>一切</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일절</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>車輛</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>차량</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>飛行機</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비행기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>船舶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>선박</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>識別</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>식별</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>標識</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>표식</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>發給</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>발급</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>26. <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監視</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>任務</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임무</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>非武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>地帶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>漢江</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>한강</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>河口</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>하구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>執行</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>집행</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>함을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協助</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 것이다

grade60"><rb>行</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>행</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>權限</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>권한</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 가진다
</p><p>29. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>違反</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위반</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>事件</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사건</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>發生</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>발생</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하였다고 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>確定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>확정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 때에는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>卽時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>즉시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 그 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>違反</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위반</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>事件</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사건</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들에게 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>30. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 어떠한 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>違反</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위반</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>事件</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사건</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>滿足</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>만족</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하게 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>是正</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>되었다고 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>確定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>확정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 때에는 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들에게 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p>
<h5><span id="3._總則(총칙)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="3._.E7.B8.BD.E5.89.87.28.EC.B4.9D.EC.B9.99.29">3. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>總則</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>총칙</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="부분 편집: 3. 總則(총칙)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>31. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>每日</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>매일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>會議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>회의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 연다  <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>首席</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수석</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>合意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>합의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>七</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>칠</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(7) <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>日</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 넘지 않는 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>休會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>휴회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 할 수 있다  <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>但</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>단</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 어느 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>一方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>首席</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수석</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이던지 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>二十四</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이십사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(24) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>時間</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시간</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>前</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>通告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로써 이 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>休會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>휴회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 끝낼 수 있다
</p><p>32. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>一切</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일절</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>會議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>회의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>記錄</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기록</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>副本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>每番</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>매번</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>會議後</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>회의후</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 될 수 있는 대로 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>速</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>히 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들에게 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送付</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다.
</p><p>33. <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監視</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>要求</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>요구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>定期</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 또 이 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들이 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>必要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>필요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하다고 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>認定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하거나 또는 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>洞</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>要求</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>요구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>特別</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>특별</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>34. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>會議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>회의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>記錄</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기록</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>文件綴</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문건철</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 두벌을 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>保管</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 그 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>事業</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사업</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>進行</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>진행</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>必要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>필요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>其他</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기타</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>記錄等</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기록등</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>文件綴</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문건철</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 두벌을 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>保管</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>權限</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>권한</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 가진다  <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>最後</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>최후</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>解散時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해산시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>上記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>상기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>文件綴</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문건철</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 한벌씩 나누어 준다
</p><p>35. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들에게 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>修正</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 또는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>增補</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>증보</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>建議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>건의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 수 있다  이러한 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>改正</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>개정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>建議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>건의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>一般的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일반적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 더 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>有效</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>유효</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>保障</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 것을 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>目的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>목적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 하는 것이어야 한다
</p>
<h4><span id="다._中立國(중립국)_監督(감독)_委員會(위원회)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".EB.8B.A4._.E4.B8.AD.E7.AB.8B.E5.9C.8B.28.EC.A4.91.EB.A6.BD.EA.B5.AD.29_.E7.9B.A3.E7.9D.A3.28.EA.B0.90.EB.8F.85.29_.E5.A7.94.E5.93.A1.E6.9C.83.28.EC.9C.84.EC.9B.90.ED.9A.8C.29">다. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="부분 편집: 다. 中立國(중립국) 監督(감독) 委員會(위원회)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span id="1._構成(구성)_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1._.E6.A7.8B.E6.88.90.28.EA.B5.AC.EC.84.B1.29_2">1. <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>構成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="부분 편집: 1. 構成(구성)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>36. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>設立</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>설립</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>37. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>四</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(4) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>高級</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>고급</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>軍官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>構成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하되 그 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>二</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(2) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>人民軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인민군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>最高</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>최고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>人民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>志願軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지원군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja <h5><span id="2._職責(직책)과_權限(권한)_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2._.E8.81.B7.E8.B2.AC.28.EC.A7.81.EC.B1.85.29.EA.B3.BC_.E6.AC.8A.E9.99.90.28.EA.B6.8C.ED.95.9C.29_2">2. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>職責</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>직책</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>權限</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>권한</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="부분 편집: 2. 職責(직책)과 權限(권한)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>

</p><p>42. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는

<p>이 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>視察</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시찰</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들은 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>添附</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>첨부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>地圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>標示</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>표시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>地域</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지역</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>內</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>내</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>交通線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>교통선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에서 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>通行上</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통행상</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>充分</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>충분</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>便利</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>편리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 받는다 (<ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>添附</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>첨부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>地圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>5<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 보라)
</p>
<h5><span id="3._總則(총칙)_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="3._.E7.B8.BD.E5.89.87.28.EC.B4.9D.EC.B9.99.29_2">3. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>總則</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>총칙</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="부분 편집: 3. 總則(총칙)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>44. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>每日</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>매일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>會議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>회의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 연다  <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>合意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>합의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>七</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>칠</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(7) <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>日</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 넘지 않는 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>休會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>휴회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 할 수 있다  <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>但</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>단</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 어느 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이던지 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>二十四</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이십사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(24) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>時間</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시간</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>前</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>通告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로써 이 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>休會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>휴회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 끝낼 수 있다
</p><p>45. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>一切</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일절</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>會議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>회의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>記錄</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기록</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>副本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>每番</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>매번</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>會議後</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>회의후</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 될 수 있는대로 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>速</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>히 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送付</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>記錄</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기록</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>中國文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중국문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>英文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>영문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>作成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>작성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>46. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>視察</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시찰</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 그의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監視</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>視察</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시찰</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>調査</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>結果</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>결과</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>要求</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>요구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>定期</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 또 이 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들이 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>必要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>필요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하다고 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>認定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하거나 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>要求</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>요구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>特別</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>특별</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  보고는 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>總體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>총체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>但</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>단</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 그 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>個別的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>개별적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>組員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>一</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(1) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 또는 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>數名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 수도 있다  <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>數名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 다만 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>參考的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>참고적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>看做</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>간주</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>47. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>視察</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시찰</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>小組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>副本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 그가 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>接受</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>접수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>使用</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>된 글로써 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>遲滯</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>없이 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送付</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  이러한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>飜譯</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>번역</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 또는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>審議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>심의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>決定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>결정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>手續</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 때문에 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>遲滯</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>시킬 수 없다  <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>實際</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>실제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>可能</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>가능</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>限</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>한</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>速</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>히 이러한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>審議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>심의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>決定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>결정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 그의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>判定書</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>판정서</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>于先</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>우선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送付</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>된 어떠한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報告</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja </p><p>48. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>必要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>필요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>其他</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기타</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja
