grade62"><rb>各</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 한벌씩 나누어 준다
</p><p>49. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>修正</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 또는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>增補</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>증보</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>建議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>건의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 수 있다  이러한 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>改正</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>개정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>建議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>건의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>一般的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일반적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 더 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>有效</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>유효</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>保障</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 것을 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>目的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>목적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 하는 것이어야 한다
</p><p>50. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 또는 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>每個</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>매개</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>任意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>通信</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통신</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>連絡</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>연락</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>련락</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>取</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>취</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>權限</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>권한</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 가진다

<h3><span id="第(제)3條(조)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.293.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>3<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="부분 편집: 第(제)3條(조)">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><big><b><ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>措置</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조치</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></b></big>
</p><p>51. <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>效力</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>효력</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>發生</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>발생</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>當時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>당시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>收容</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하고 있는 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>全體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>釋放</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>석방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>調印</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조인</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>前</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>合意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>합의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>下記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>하기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 따라 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>執行</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>집행</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>ㄱ. <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>效力</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>효력</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>發生</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>발생</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>後</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>후</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>六十</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>육십</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>륙십</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(60) <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>日</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>以內</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이내</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 그 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>收容下</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수용하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 있는 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>構成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하되 그<ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>二</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(2) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>人民軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인민군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>最高</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>최고</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>人民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>志願軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지원군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>任命</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 그<ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>二</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(2) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>聯合國軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>연합국군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>련합국군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>總</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>총</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>全般的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전반적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>指導</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 밑에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>責任</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>책임</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>지고 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>上記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>상기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>私民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>歸鄕</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>귀향</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協助</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는데 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>關係</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관계</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>되는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>具體的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구체적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>計劃</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>계획</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>調節</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조절</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 또 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>上記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>상기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>私民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>歸鄕</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>귀향</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>關係</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관계</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>되는 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>執行</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>집행</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 것을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>任務</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임무</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>移動</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>促進</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>촉진</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>調節</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조절</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>上記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>상기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>私民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>越境地點</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>월경지점</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(들)을 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>選定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>선정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>完了</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>완료</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하기 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>爲</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja </p><p>(2) <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>失鄕</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>실향</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>私民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 그의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>任務</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임무</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>關係</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관계</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>되는 어떠한 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>事項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이던지 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>合意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>합의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>到達</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도달</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 수 없을 때에는 이를 곧 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>提出</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제출</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>決定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>결정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하게 한다  <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>失鄕</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>실향</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>私民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>歸鄕</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>귀향</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協助</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 그의 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本部</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本部</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>附近</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부근</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>設置</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>설치</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>(3) <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>失鄕</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>실향</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>私民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>歸鄕</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>귀향</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協助</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 그의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>任務</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임무</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>完遂</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>완수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 때에는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>卽時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>즉시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 이를 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>解散</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해산</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>시킨다

<h3><span id="第(제)4條(조)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.294.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>4<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="부분 편집: 第(제)4條(조)">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><big><b><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>關係</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관계</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>政府</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들에의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>建議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>건의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></b></big>
</p><p>60. <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>問題</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>平和的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>평화적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解決</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해결</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>保障</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하기 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>爲</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>關係</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관계</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>政府</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>調印</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조인</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>되고 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>效力</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>효력</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>發生</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>발생</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>後</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>후</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>三</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>삼</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(3) <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>個月</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>개월</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>內</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>내</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>各其</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>代表</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대표</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>派遣</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>파견</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 한<ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>級</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>급</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 높은 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>政治</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정치</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>會議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>회의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>召集</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소집</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하고 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로부터의 모든 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>外國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>외국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>軍隊</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>撤去</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>철거</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>問題</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>平和的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>평화적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解決</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해결</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>等</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>등</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>問題</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 것을 이에 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>建議</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>건의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p>
<h3><span id="第(제)5條(조)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.295.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>5<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="부분 편집: 第(제)5條(조)">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><big><b><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>附則</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부칙</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></b></big>
</p><p>61. <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>修正</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>增補</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>증보</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 반드시 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>敵對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>司令官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사령관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들의 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>互相</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>호상</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>合意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>합의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 거처야 한다
</p><p>62. <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>條項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>共同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>接受</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>접수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>修正</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>增補</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>증보</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 또는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>政治的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정치적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>水準</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수준</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에서의 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>平和的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>평화적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解決</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해결</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>爲</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>適當</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적당</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>依</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>明確</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명확</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>히 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>交替</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>교체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>될 때까지는 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>繼續</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>계속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>效力</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>효력</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 가진다
</p><p>63. <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>12<ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>除外</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제외</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>一切</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일절</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 1953<ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>年</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>년</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 7<ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>月</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>월</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 27<ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>日</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 2200<ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>부터 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>效力</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>효력</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>發生</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>발생</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>1953<ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>年</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>년</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 7<ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>月</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>월</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 27<ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>日</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 1000<ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>板門店</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>판문점</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에서 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>中國文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중국문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>英文</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>영문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로써 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>作成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>작성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  이 세가지 글의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>文本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>同等</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동등</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>效力</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>효력</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 가진다
</p>

<h3><span id="附錄(부록)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E9.99.84.E9.8C.84.28.EB.B6.80.EB.A1.9D.29"><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>附錄</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부록</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="부분 편집: 附錄(부록)">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><big><b><ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>職權</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>직권</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>範圍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>범위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></b></big>
</p><p>(<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>51<ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> ㄴ<ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>目</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>목</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 보라)
</p>
<h4><span id="第(제)1條(조)_總則(총칙)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.291.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29_.E7.B8.BD.E5.89.87.28.EC.B4.9D.EC.B9.99.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>1<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>總則</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>총칙</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="부분 편집: 第(제)1條(조) 總則(총칙)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>1. <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>全體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 하여금 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>後</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>후</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>被</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>피</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還權</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환권</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>行使</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>행사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>機會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 가지도록 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>保障</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하기 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>爲</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>雙方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>쌍방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>波蘭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>파란</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 체코슬로바키야 <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>瑞典</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>서전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>瑞西</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>서서</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>印度</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各各</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각각</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>一</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(1) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>씩의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>任命</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하도록 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>要請</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>요청</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>設立</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>설립</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하고 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>抑留側</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>억류측</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>下</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 있는 동안 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>被</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>피</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還權</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환권</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>行使</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>행사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하지 않은 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에서 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>收容</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 그 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本部</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>非</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>地帶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>內</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>내</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>板門店</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>판문점</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>附近</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부근</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 두며 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>構成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 가진 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>從屬</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>종속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>地點</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지점</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>駐在</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>주재</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>시킨다  <ruby class="hanja <p>4. <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>以後</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이후</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>可能</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>가능</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>限</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>한</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>速</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>히 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>最大限</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>최대한</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>六十</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>육십</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>륙십</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(60) <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>日</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby grade32"><rb>側</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>측</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>統制</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>收容</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>下</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로부터 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>釋放</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>석방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>되어 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>抑留</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>억류</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>側</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>측</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>指定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>內</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>내</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>地區</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에서 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 넘어 간다
</p><p>5. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>收容</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>施設</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시설</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>責任</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>책임</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 맡을 때에 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>抑留側</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>억류측</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>部隊</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>부대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 그곳에서 <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>撤收</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>철수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>함으로써 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>前項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>地區</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>印度</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>力量</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>역량</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>력량</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 하여금 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>全的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>接收</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>접수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>케 한다
</p><p>6. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>上記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>상기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>5<ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>不拘</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>불구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하고 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>抑留</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>억류</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>地區</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>周邊</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>주변</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>保障</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>抑留</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>억류</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>側</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>측</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>地區</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>團束</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>단속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>責任</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>책임</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 진다
</p><p>7. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>上記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>상기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>3<ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>不拘</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>불구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하고 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>如何</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>여하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja class="hanja grade32"><rb>臨時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>림시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>管轄下</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관할하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 있는 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>統制</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>責任</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>책임</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>執行</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>집행</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>權限</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>권한</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>弱化</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>약화</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>시키는 것으로 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>解釋</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해석</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 수 없다

<h4><span id="第(제)3條(조)_解說(해설)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.293.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29_.E8.A7.A3.E8.AA.AA.28.ED.95.B4.EC.84.A4.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>3<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解說</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해설</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="부분 편집: 第(제)3條(조) 解說(해설)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>8. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>被</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>피</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還權</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환권</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>行使</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>행사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하지 않은 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>全體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>接收</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>접수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하게 된<ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>後</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>후</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>卽時</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>즉시</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>措置</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조치</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>取</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>취</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>所屬</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소속</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>國家</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>국가</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>들로 하여금 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>自由</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>자유</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>便利</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>편리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 가지고 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>接收</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>접수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하게 된 날부터 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>九十</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구십</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(90) <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>日</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>以內</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이내</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>下記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>하기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 따라 이러한 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>地區</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>代表</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대표</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>派遣</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>파견</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>同</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>所屬國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>소속국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>依託</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>의탁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>全體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에게 그들의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>權利</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>권리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解說</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해설</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 그들이 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>故鄕</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>고향</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 도라가는 데 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>關聯</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관련</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>되는 모든 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>事項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>特</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>특</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>히 그들이 집에 도라가 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>平和的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>평화적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>生活</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>생활</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 할 수 있는 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>完全</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>완전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>自由</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>자유</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 가지고 있다는 것을 알리게 한다
</p><p>ㄱ. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解說</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해설</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>從事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>종사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 이러한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>代表</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대표</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>數爻</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수효</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理下</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 있는 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>每</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>매</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>千</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>천</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(1,000) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>七</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>칠</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(7) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 넘지 못하되 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>許諾</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>허락</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>될 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>最低</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>최저</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>總數</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>총수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>五</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>오</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(5) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>以下</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 되어서는 안된다
</p><p>ㄴ. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解說</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해설</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>從事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>종사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>代表</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대표</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에게 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>接近</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>접근</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>時間</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시간</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>決定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>결정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>大體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>待遇</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대우</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 제네바 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協約</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협약</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>53<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>依據</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>의거</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>ㄷ. <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>一切</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일절</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解說</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해설</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>事業</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사업</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>面會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>면회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>成員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>성원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>國家</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>국가</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>代表</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대표</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>一</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(1) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>씩과 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>抑留</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>억류</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>側</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>측</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>代表</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대표</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>一</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(1) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>立會下</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>입회하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>립회하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>進行</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>진행</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p><p>ㄹ. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解說</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해설</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>事業</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사업</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>追加的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>추가적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>制定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>上記</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>상기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>3<ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>과 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>本項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>列擧</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>열거</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>렬거</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>原則</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>원칙</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>適用</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 것을 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>目的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>목적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 한다
</p><p>ㅁ. <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>解說</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>해설</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>從事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>종사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>許容</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>허용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>通信</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통신</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>人員</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>數爻</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수효</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>一</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(1) <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 씩으로 <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>戰爭捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 한 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>地區</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>組</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>許諾</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>허락</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다  <ruby class="hanja <h4><span id="第(제)4條(조)_戰爭(전쟁)_捕虜(포로)의_處理(처리)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.294.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29_.E6.88.B0.E7.88.AD.28.EC.A0.84.EC.9F.81.29_.E6.8D.95.E8.99.9C.28.ED.8F.AC.EB.A1.9C.29.EC.9D.98_.E8.99.95.E7.90.86.28.EC.B2.98.EB.A6.AC.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>4<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>處理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>처리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="부분 편집: 第(제)4條(조) 戰爭(전쟁) 捕虜(포로)의 處理(처리)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>10. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理下</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 있는 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 누구나 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>被</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>피</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還權</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환권</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>行使</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>행사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하기로 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>決定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>결정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하면 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>成員國家</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>성원국가</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>代表</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대표</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>一</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>(1) <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>씩으로써 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>構成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja <h4><span id="第(제)5條(조)_赤十字社(적십자사)의_訪問(방문)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.295.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29_.E8.B5.A4.E5.8D.81.E5.AD.97.E7.A4.BE.28.EC.A0.81.EC.8B.AD.EC.9E.90.EC.82.AC.29.EC.9D.98_.E8.A8.AA.E5.95.8F.28.EB.B0.A9.EB.AC.B8.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>5<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>赤十字社</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적십자사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>訪問</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>방문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="부분 편집: 第(제)5條(조) 赤十字社(적십자사)의 訪問(방문)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>12. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>管理</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관리</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>下</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 있는 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에게 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>必要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>필요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>赤十字社</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>적십자사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>服務</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>복무</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>發表</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>발표</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>規則</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>규칙</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>依</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>印度</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>인도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>提供</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제공</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다
</p>
<h4><span id="第(제)6條(조)_新聞報道(신문보도)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.296.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29_.E6.96.B0.E8.81.9E.E5.A0.B1.E9.81.93.28.EC.8B.A0.EB.AC.B8.EB.B3.B4.EB.8F.84.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>6<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>新聞報道</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>신문보도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="부분 편집: 第(제)6條(조) 新聞報道(신문보도)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>13. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>制定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>節次</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>절차</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>依</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>新聞界</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>신문계</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>其他</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기타</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>報道</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>機關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>列擧</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>열거</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>렬거</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>全體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>事業</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사업</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>參觀</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>참관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>自由</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>자유</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 가지도록 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>保障</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다

<h4><span id="第(제)7條(조)_戰爭(전쟁)_捕虜(포로)를_爲(위)한_補給(보급)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.297.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29_.E6.88.B0.E7.88.AD.28.EC.A0.84.EC.9F.81.29_.E6.8D.95.E8.99.9C.28.ED.8F.AC.EB.A1.9C.29.EB.A5.BC_.E7.88.B2.28.EC.9C.84.29.ED.95.9C_.E8.A3.9C.E7.B5.A6.28.EB.B3.B4.EA.B8.89.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>7<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>戰爭</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>전쟁</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade10"><rb>捕虜</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포로</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>爲</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>補給</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보급</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="부분 편집: 第(제)7條(조) 戰爭(전쟁) 捕虜(포로)를 爲(위)한 補給(보급)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>14. <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>各方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>각방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>自己</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>자기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja </p><p>17. <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>收容</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>수용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>施設</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>시설</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>로 돌려보낸다
</p>
<h4><span id="第(제)8條(조)_中立國(중립국)_送還(송환)_委員會(위원회)를_爲(위)한_補給(보급)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.298.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29_.E4.B8.AD.E7.AB.8B.E5.9C.8B.28.EC.A4.91.EB.A6.BD.EA.B5.AD.29_.E9.80.81.E9.82.84.28.EC.86.A1.ED.99.98.29_.E5.A7.94.E5.93.A1.E6.9C.83.28.EC.9C.84.EC.9B.90.ED.9A.8C.29.EB.A5.BC_.E7.88.B2.28.EC.9C.84.29.ED.95.9C_.E8.A3.9C.E7.B5.A6.28.EB.B3.B4.EA.B8.89.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>8<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>中立國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중립국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>送還</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>송환</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>爲</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>補給</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보급</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="부분 편집: 第(제)8條(조) 中立國(중립국) 送還(송환) 委員會(위원회)를 爲(위)한 補給(보급)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h4><span id="第(제)9條(조)_發表(발표)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.299.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29_.E7.99.BC.E8.A1.A8.28.EB.B0.9C.ED.91.9C.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>9<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>發表</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>발표</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="부분 편집: 第(제)9條(조) 發表(발표)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h4><span id="第(제)10條(조)_移動(이동)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.2910.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29_.E7.A7.BB.E5.8B.95.28.EC.9D.B4.EB.8F.99.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>10<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>移動</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이동</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="부분 편집: 第(제)10條(조) 移動(이동)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h4><span id="第(제)11條(조)_節次(절차)에_關(관)한_事項(사항)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E7.AC.AC.28.EC.A0.9C.2911.E6.A2.9D.28.EC.A1.B0.29_.E7.AF.80.E6.AC.A1.28.EC.A0.88.EC.B0.A8.29.EC.97.90_.E9.97.9C.28.EA.B4.80.29.ED.95.9C_.E4.BA.8B.E9.A0.85.28.EC.82.AC.ED.95.AD.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>11<ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>條</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>節次</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>절차</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>事項</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="부분 편집: 第(제)11條(조) 節次(절차)에 關(관)한 事項(사항)&nbsp;">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h2><span id="地圖(지도)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E5.9C.B0.E5.9C.96.28.EC.A7.80.EB.8F.84.29"><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>地圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="부분 편집: 地圖(지도)">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>停戰協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 <ruby class="hanja grade30"><rb>添附地圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>첨부지도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 다섯 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>張</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>包含</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>포함</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한다.
</p>
<ul><li><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>1<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>: <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>分界線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>분계선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 및 <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>非武裝</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>비무장</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>地帶</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의&nbsp;<ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>北</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>북</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>經界線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>경계선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와 <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>南</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>남</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>經界線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>경계선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></li>
<li><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>2<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>: <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>軍事</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>군사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>委員會</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>위원회</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>監督下</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>감독하</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>漢江口</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>한강구</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>區域</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>구역</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></li>
<li><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>3<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>: <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>朝鮮</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>조선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>西部</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>서부</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>沿海</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>연해</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> 섬들의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>統制</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></li>
<li><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>4<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>: <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>主要</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>주요</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>交通線</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>교통선</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></li>
<li><ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>第</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>제</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>5<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>圖</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>도</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>: <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>出入港</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>출입항</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></li></ul>
<h2><span id="停戰協定(정전협정)에_對(대)한_臨時的(임시적)(림시적)_補充(보충)_協定(협정)[10]"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E5.81.9C.E6.88.B0.E5.8D.94.E5.AE.9A.28.EC.A0.95.EC.A0.84.ED.98.91.EC.A0.95.29.EC.97.90_.E5.B0.8D.28.EB.8C.80.29.ED.95.9C_.E8.87.A8.E6.99.82.E7.9A.84.28.EC.9E.84.EC.8B.9C.EC.A0.81.29.28.EB.A6.BC.EC.8B.9C.EC.A0.81.29_.E8.A3.9C.E5.85.85.28.EB.B3.B4.EC.B6.A9.29_.E5.8D.94.E5.AE.9A.28.ED.98.91.EC.A0.95.29.5B10.5D"><ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>停戰協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade0"><rb><span class="noruby"><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>臨時的</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>임시적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span></rb><rp>(</rp><rt>림시적</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>補充</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>보충</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">[10]</a></sup><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="부분 편집: 停戰協定(정전협정)에 對(대)한 臨時的(임시적)(림시적) 補充(보충) 協定(협정)[10]">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h2><span id="其他(기타)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id=".E5.85.B6.E4.BB.96.28.EA.B8.B0.ED.83.80.29"><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>其他</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기타</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/index.php?title=%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E5%81%9C%E6%88%B0%E5%8D%94%E5%AE%9A&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="부분 편집: 其他(기타)">편집</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>이 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>文書</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>문서</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <a href="/wiki/%E9%9F%93%E5%9C%8B%E8%AA%9E" title="韓國語"><ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>韓國語</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>한국어</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></a><ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>版</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>판</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>寫本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>中</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>중</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>&nbsp;<a href="/index.php?title=%E5%85%AC%E4%B8%99%E7%A6%B9_%E6%89%93%E5%AD%97%E6%A9%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="公丙禹 打字機 (없는 문서)"><ruby class="hanja grade12 unknown"><rb>公丙禹</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공병우</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40 unknown"><rb>打字機</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>타자기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></a>로 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>作成</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>작성</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>된 것이 있다. 그 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>寫本</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>사본</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에서 <a href="/wiki/%E6%98%8E%E6%9C%9D%E9%AB%94" title="明朝體"><ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>明朝體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>명조체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></a>가 아닌 둥글둥글한 <a href="/wiki/%EA%B3%A0%EB%94%95%E9%AB%94" title="고딕體">고딕<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby></a> <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>基盤</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>기반</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>草創期</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>초창기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade12"><rb>公丙禹</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공병우</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade40"><rb>打字機</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>타자기</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>書體</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>서체</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>確認</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>확인</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 수 있다.</li>
<li><ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>當時大韓民國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>당시대한민국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의<ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>大統領</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대통령</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이자<ruby class="hanja grade80"><rb>大韓民國國軍</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대한민국국군</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의<ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>統帥權者</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>통수권자</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>였던, <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>李承晩博士</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>이승만박사</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는<ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>停戰協定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전협정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이<ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>署名</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>서명</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하지않았다. 이는<ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>當時大韓民國民</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>당시대한민국민</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의<ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>大多數</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>대다수</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>는<ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>停戰</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>정전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에<ruby class="hanja grade62"><rb>反對</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>반대</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하며, <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>共産主義</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>공산주의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>와<ruby class="hanja grade20"><rb>北傀</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>북괴</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를<ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>完全</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>완전</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>히<ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>滅</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>멸</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하는<ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>形式</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>형식</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의<ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>北進統一</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>북진통일</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>을<ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>願</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>원</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하였기때문이다.</li></ul>

grade42"><rb>要請</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>요청</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>이 있을 때에는 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>關係國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관계국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>方法</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>방법</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>으로 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>審問</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>심문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여야 한다. <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>審問</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>심문</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>節次</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>절차</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>한 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>合意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>합의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>가 이루어지지 아니하였을 때는 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>關係國</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관계국</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>은 그 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>節次</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>절차</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>를 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>決定</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>결정</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>할 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>審判官</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>심판관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade50"><rb>選任</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>선임</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에 <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>關</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>관</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여 <ruby class="hanja grade60"><rb>合意</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>합의</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하여야 한다.”</span>
</li>

grade30"><rb>當該</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>당해</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade70"><rb>地方</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>지방</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>의 <ruby class="hanja grade72"><rb>民間人</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>민간인</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby> <ruby class="hanja grade52"><rb>勞動者</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>노동자</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>에게 <ruby class="hanja grade42"><rb>許容</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>허용</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>되는 바를 <ruby class="hanja grade32"><rb>超過</rb><rp>(</rp><rt>초과</rt><rp>)</rp></ruby>하지 못한다. <ruby class="hanja
